START).astype(int)\nevt['weekday'] = evt['dt'].dt.dayofweek\nevt['month'] = evt['dt'].dt.month\nevt = evt.sort_values(['store_id','product_id','day','dt'])\nevt = evt.groupby(['store_id','product_id','day'], as_index=False).tail(1)[['visit_id','store_id','product_id','rep_id','visit_type','dt','day','weekday','month']]\nevt = evt.sort_values(['store_id','product_id','day','dt']).reset_index(drop=True)\nevt['next_day'] = evt.groupby(['store_id','product_id'])['day'].shift(-1)\nevt['prev_day'] = evt.groupby(['store_id','product_id'])['day'].shift(1)\nevt['pair_idx'] = (evt['store_id'].to_numpy()-1)*N_PRODUCTS + (evt['product_id'].to_numpy()-1)\nevt = evt.merge(rep_meta, on='rep_id', how='left').merge(comp_agg, on='visit_id', how='left')\nevt[['comp_facings','comp_brands']] = evt[['comp_facings','comp_brands']].fillna(0)\nevt['comp_promo'] = evt['comp_promo'].fillna(False).astype(int)\n\nnext_day = evt['next_day'].fillna(N_DAYS).to_numpy()\nday = evt['day'].to_numpy()\nL = np.minimum(7, np.maximum(0, next_day - before_disc\nevt['L'] = L\nevt['log_prev_gap'] = np.log1p(prev_gap)\n\n# Fit control-only model with region effects\nX = pd.get_dummies(evt[['visit_type','month','weekday','region']], columns=['visit_type','month','weekday','region'], drop_first=True, dtype=float)\nfor c in ['log_pre_mean','traffic_diff','promo_diff','disc_diff','L','log_prev_gap','comp_facings','comp_brands','comp_promo']:\n    X[c] = evt[c].astype(float).to_numpy()\nX = sm.add_constant(X, has_constant='add')\nmodel = sm.OLS(evt['y'].to_numpy(), X.to_numpy()).fit()\nevt['resid'] = model.resid\n\n# rep tests vs region peers\nrows=[]\nfor region, g in evt.groupby('region'):\n    for rep_id, gr in g.groupby('rep_id'):\n        others = g[g['rep_id'] \"'!= rep_id]['\"'resid']\n        m1 = gr['resid'].mean(); m0 = others.mean()\n        v1 = gr['resid'].var(ddof=1); v0 = others.var(ddof=1)\n        n1 = len(gr); n0 = len(others)\n        se = np.sqrt(v1/n1 + v0/n0)\n        t = (m1 - m0) / se\n        rows.append({'region':region,'rep_id':rep_id,'n':n1,'mean_resid':m1,'diff_vs_region_others':m1-m0,'t_vs_others':t})\nres = pd.DataFrame(rows).sort_values('diff_vs_region_others')\nprint('control model r2', model.rsquared)\nprint(res.head(20).round(4).to_string(index=False))\nPY\"","aggregated_output":"","exit_code":null,"status":"in_progress"}}
